[30;1m277 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m278 | [0m[35mTo invoke ``set_keyring``::[0m
[30;1m279 | [0m[35m[0m

[31m--[ [0m[34mMatch #[0m[33m417[0m[34m of [0m[33m820[0m[31m ]--[0m

   Pattern: [32m(npm owner|password|htpasswd|auth_?token|secret_?key|private_?key|authorized_keys?|npmrc|\.ssh|usersecrets?|api_?keys|nuget\.config|\.identityservice)[0m
[30;1m249 | [0m[35mThe interface for the backend is defined by ``keyring.backend.KeyringBackend``.[0m
[30;1m250 | [0m[35mEvery backend should derive from that base class and define a ``priority``[0m

[30;1m252 | [0m[35m``delete_password()``. The ``get_credential()`` function may be defined if[0m
[30;1m253 | [0m[35mdesired.[0m
[30;1m254 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m255 | [0m[35mSee the ``backend`` module for more detail on the interface of this class.[0m

[30;1m1484 | [0m[35m  2.[0m
[30;1m1485 | [0m[35m* CryptedFileKeyring now uses PBKDF2 to derive the key from the user's[0m
[30;1m1486 | [0m[35m  password and a random hash. The IV is chosen randomly as well. All the[0m
[30;1m1487 | [0m[35m  stored passwords are encrypted at once. Any keyrings using the old format[0m
[30;1m1488 | [0m[35m  will be automatically converted to the new format (but will no longer be[0m
[30;1m1489 | [0m[35m  compatible with 0.9 and earlier). The user's password is no longer limited[0m
[30;1m1490 | [0m[35m  to 32 characters. PyCrypto 2.5 or greater is now required for this keyring.[0m
